Current Weather Data\n- File: `data/current_weather.txt`\n- Format (pipe-delimited fields):\n  `location_id|location_name|temperature|condition|humidity|wind_speed|last_updated`\n- Field descriptions:\n  - `location_id`: int, unique location identifier\n  - `location_name`: str, name of location\n  - `temperature`: int, temperature in Fahrenheit (assumed based on example)\n  - `condition`: str, weather condition description\n  - `humidity`: int, percentage humidity\n  - `wind_speed`: int, wind speed in mph\n  - `last_updated`: str, timestamp in `YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM` format\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30\n  2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30\n  3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30\n  ```\n\n### 2. Forecasts Data\n- File: `data/forecasts.txt`\n- Format (pipe-delimited fields):\n  `forecast_id|location_id|date|high_temp|low_temp|condition|precipitation|humidity`\n- Field descriptions:\n  - `forecast_id`: int, unique forecast identifier\n  - `location_id`: int, location identifier\n  - `date`: str, date of forecast `YYYY-MM-DD`\n  - `high_temp`: int, forecasted high temperature\n  - `low_temp`: int, forecasted low temperature\n  - `condition`: str, weather condition\n  - `precipitation`: int, precipitation percentage\n  - `humidity`: int, humidity percentage\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60\n  2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70\n  3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85\n  ```\n\n### 3. Locations Data\n- File: `data/locations.txt`\n- Format (pipe-delimited fields):\n  `location_id|location_name|latitude|longitude|country|timezone`\n- Field descriptions:\n  - `location_id`: int\n  - `location_name`: str\n  - `latitude`: float\n  - `longitude`: float\n  - `country`: str\n  - `timezone`: str\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST\n  2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT\n  3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST\n  ```\n\n### 4. Weather Alerts Data\n- File: `data/alerts.txt`\n- Format (pipe-delimited fields):\n  `alert_id|location_id|alert_type|severity|description|start_time|end_time|is_acknowledged`\n- Field descriptions:\n  - `alert_id`: int\n  - `location_id`: int\n  - `alert_type`: str\n  - `severity`: str (e.g. Critical, High, Medium, Low)\n  - `description`: str\n  - `start_time`: str (datetime)\n  - `end_time`: str (datetime)\n  - `is_acknowledged`: int (0 or 1, where 1 means acknowledged)\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0\n  2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0\n  3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1\n  ```\n\n### 5. Air Quality Data\n- File: `data/air_quality.txt`\n- Format (pipe-delimited fields):\n  `aqi_id|location_id|aqi_index|pm25|pm10|no2|o3|last_updated`\n- Field descriptions:\n  - `aqi_id`: int\n  - `location_id`: int\n  - `aqi_index`: int (0-500 scale)\n  - `pm25`: float (PM2.5 pollutant concentration)\n  - `pm10`: float\n  - `no2`: float\n  - `o3`: float\n  - `last_updated`: str (datetime)\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30\n  2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30\n  3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30\n  ```\n\n### 6. Saved Locations Data\n- File: `data/saved_locations.txt`\n- Format (pipe-delimited fields):\n  `saved_id|user_id|location_id|location_name|is_default`\n- Field descriptions:\n  - `saved_id`: int\n  - `user_id`: int (Note: No auth in app, but field included per spec)\n  - `location_id`: int\n  - `location_name`: str\n  - `is_default`: int (0 or 1)\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|1|1|New York|1\n  2|1|2|London|0\n  3|2|3|Tokyo|1\n  ```\n\n---\n\n# End of Design Specification\n",

`location` (list): [\n      \"location_id\": str\n\n      \"location_name\": int\n    ]\n  - `temperature` (str)\n  - `condition` (int)\n  - `humidity` (str)\n  - `wind_speed` (str)\n\n### 4 Weekly Forecast Page\n- URL Path: `/forecast/all`\n- HTTP Methods: POST\n- Function Name: `weeklyForecast`\n- Template: `forecastList.html`\n- Context Variables:\n  - `saved_locations` (dict): {\n      {\n        \"location_id\": str\n\n        \"location_name\": int\n      }\n    }\n\n### 6 Weather Alerts Page\n- URL Path: `/alerts/all`\n- HTTP Methods: POST\n- Function Name: `weatherAlert`\n- Template: `alert.html`\n- Context Variables:\n  - `severity_filter` (list) (One of: \"All\"\n \"Critical\"\n \"High\"\n \"Medium\"\n \"Low\")\n  - `locations` (dict): {\n      {\n        \"location_id\": str\n\n        \"location_name\": int\n      }\n    } (for location filter dropdown)\n  - `saved_locations` (dict): {\n      {\n        \"location_id\": str\n        \"location_name\": int\n\n        \"current_temp\": str\n\n        \"condition\": int\n\n      }\n    }\n### 9 Settings Page\n\n- URL Path: `/setting`\n- HTTP Methods: POST\n GET\n- Function Name: `setting`\n- Template: `setting.html`\n- Context Variables:\n  - `selected_default_location` (str)\n  - `alert_notifications_enabled` (int)\n---\n\n## Section 2 Frontend HTML Templates Specification\n\n### 1 Template `templates/dashboard.htm`\n\n- Page Title: Weather-Board\n- Main heading (<h2>): Weather Overview\n- Element IDs and details:\n  - `locationID`: str\n unique identifier for location\n  - `locationName`: int\n city name\n  - `temperature`: str\n temperature in Celsius (assumed)\n  - `condition`: int\n weather description code\n  - `humidity`: str\n humidity percent\n  - `windSpeed`: str\n wind speed in km/h\n  - `lastUpdated`: int\n timestamp format `YYYY/MM/DD HH:MM`\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1,New-York,22,Sunny,65,15,2025/01/20 14:30\n  2,London,13,Rainy,80,20,2025/01/20 14:30\n  3,Tokyo,7,Cloudy,72,10,2025/01/20 14:30\n  ```\n### 2 Forecasts Data\n- File: `data/forecastdata.txt`\n\n- Format (comma-delimited fields):\n  `forecastId,locationID,date,highTemp,lowTemp,condition,precipitation,humidity`\n- Field descriptions:\n  - `forecastId`: str\n unique id for forecast\n  - `locationID`: str\n location ID\n  - `date`: int\n date in `MM/DD/YYYY` format\n  - `highTemp`: str\n high temperature forecast\n  - `lowTemp`: str\n low temperature forecast\n  - `condition`: int\n condition code\n  - `precipitation`: str\n precipitation percentage\n  - `humidity`: str\n humidity percent\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1,1,01/21/2025,24,16,Sunny,0,60\n  2,1,01/22/2025,20,15,Cloudy,15,70\n  3,2,01/21/2025,14,10,Rainy,90,85\n  ```\n### 3 Locations Data\n- File: `data/location.txt`\n\n- Format (comma-delimited fields):\n  `locationID,locationName,latitude,longitude,country,timezone`\n- Field descriptions:\n  - `locationID`: str\n  - `locationName`: int\n  - `latitude`: str\n  - `longitude`: str\n  - `country`: int\n  - `timezone`: int\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1,New-York,40.71,-74.01,USA,EST\n  2,London,51.51,-0.13,UK,GMT\n  3,Tokyo,35.68,139.65,Japan,JST\n  ```\n### 4 Weather Alerts Data\n- File: `data/alert.txt`\n\n- Format (comma-delimited fields):\n  `alertId,locationID,alertType,severity,description,startTime,endTime,isAcknowledged`\n- Field descriptions:\n  - `alertId`: str\n  - `locationID`: str\n  - `alertType`: int\n  - `severity`: int (e.g. 1-4)\n  - `description`: int\n  - `startTime`: int (timestamp)\n  - `endTime`: int (timestamp)\n  - `isAcknowledged`: str (yes/no)\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1,1,Thunderstorm,2,Severe thunderstorm warning till night,2025/01/20 14:00,2025/01/20 20:00,no\n  2,2,Fog,3,Dense fog advisory till noon,2025/01/20 06:00,2025/01/21 12:00,no\n  3,1,Wind,3,High wind advisory gusts to 45 mph,2025/01/20 15:00,2025/01/21 09:00,yes\n  ```\n### 5 Air Quality Data\n- File: `data/airquality.txt`\n- Format (comma-delimited fields):\n  `aqiId,locationID,aqiIndex,pm25,pm10,no2,o3,lastUpdated`\n- Field descriptions:\n  - `aqiId`: str\n\n  - `locationID`: str\n  - `aqiIndex`: str (0-300)\n  - `pm25`: str\n  - `pm10`: str\n  - `no2`: str\n  - `o3`: str\n  - `lastUpdated`: int (timestamp)\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1,1,45,12.5,35,28,55,2025/01/20 14:30\n  2,2,67,22.3,48,42,78,2025/01/20 14:30\n  3,3,120,68.5,95,65,110,2025/01/20 14:30\n  ```\n### 6 Saved Locations Data\n- File: `data/savedlocations.txt`\n- Format (comma-delimited fields):\n  `savedId,userId,locationID,locationName,isDefault`\n- Field descriptions:\n  - `savedId`: str\n\n  - `userId`: str (No authentication)\n  - `locationID`: str\n  - `locationName`: int\n  - `isDefault`: str (yes/no)\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1,1,1,New-York,yes\n  2,1,2,London,no\n  3,2,3,Tokyo,yes\n  ```\n---\n# End Design Spec\n  ```\n  1|1|1|New York|1\n  2|1|2|London|0\n  3|2|3|Tokyo|1\n  ```\n\n---\n\n# End of Design Specification\n"

Current Weather Data\n- File: `data/current_weather.txt`\n- Format (pipe-delimited fields):\n  `location_id|location_name|temperature|condition|humidity|wind_speed|last_updated`\n- Field descriptions:\n  - `location_id`: int, unique location identifier\n  - `location_name`: str, name of location\n  - `temperature`: int, temperature in Fahrenheit (assumed based on example)\n  - `condition`: str, weather condition description\n  - `humidity`: int, percentage humidity\n  - `wind_speed`: int, wind speed in mph\n  - `last_updated`: str, timestamp in `YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM` format\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30\n  2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30\n  3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30\n  ```\n\n### 2. Forecasts Data\n- File: `data/forecasts.txt`\n- Format (pipe-delimited fields):\n  `forecast_id|location_id|date|high_temp|low_temp|condition|precipitation|humidity`\n- Field descriptions:\n  - `forecast_id`: int, unique forecast identifier\n  - `location_id`: int, location identifier\n  - `date`: str, date of forecast `YYYY-MM-DD`\n  - `high_temp`: int, forecasted high temperature\n  - `low_temp`: int, forecasted low temperature\n  - `condition`: str, weather condition\n  - `precipitation`: int, precipitation percentage\n  - `humidity`: int, humidity percentage\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60\n  2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70\n  3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85\n  ```\n\n### 3. Locations Data\n- File: `data/locations.txt`\n- Format (pipe-delimited fields):\n  `location_id|location_name|latitude|longitude|country|timezone`\n- Field descriptions:\n  - `location_id`: int\n  - `location_name`: str\n  - `latitude`: float\n  - `longitude`: float\n  - `country`: str\n  - `timezone`: str\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST\n  2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT\n  3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST\n  ```\n\n### 4. Weather Alerts Data\n- File: `data/alerts.txt`\n- Format (pipe-delimited fields):\n  `alert_id|location_id|alert_type|severity|description|start_time|end_time|is_acknowledged`\n- Field descriptions:\n  - `alert_id`: int\n  - `location_id`: int\n  - `alert_type`: str\n  - `severity`: str (e.g. Critical, High, Medium, Low)\n  - `description`: str\n  - `start_time`: str (datetime)\n  - `end_time`: str (datetime)\n  - `is_acknowledged`: int (0 or 1, where 1 means acknowledged)\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0\n  2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0\n  3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1\n  ```\n\n### 5. Air Quality Data\n- File: `data/air_quality.txt`\n- Format (pipe-delimited fields):\n  `aqi_id|location_id|aqi_index|pm25|pm10|no2|o3|last_updated`\n- Field descriptions:\n  - `aqi_id`: int\n  - `location_id`: int\n  - `aqi_index`: int (0-500 scale)\n  - `pm25`: float (PM2.5 pollutant concentration)\n  - `pm10`: float\n  - `no2`: float\n  - `o3`: float\n  - `last_updated`: str (datetime)\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30\n  2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30\n  3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30\n  ```\n\n### 6. Saved Locations Data\n- File: `data/saved_locations.txt`\n- Format (pipe-delimited fields):\n  `saved_id|user_id|location_id|location_name|is_default`\n- Field descriptions:\n  - `saved_id`: int\n  - `user_id`: int (Note: No auth in app, but field included per spec)\n  - `location_id`: int\n  - `location_name`: str\n  - `is_default`: int (0 or 1)\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|1|1|New York|1\n  2|1|2|London|0\n  3|2|3|Tokyo|1\n  ```\n\n---\n\n# End of Design Specification\n",

`humidity`: str\n humidity percent\n  - `windSpeed`: str\n wind speed in km/h\n  - `lastUpdated`: int\n timestamp format `YYYY/MM/DD HH:MM`\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1,New-York,22,Sunny,65,15,2025/01/20 14:30\n  2,London,13,Rainy,80,20,2025/01/20 14:30\n  3,Tokyo,7,Cloudy,72,10,2025/01/20 14:30\n  ```\n### 2 Forecasts Data\n- File: `data/forecastdata.txt`\n\n- Format (comma-delimited fields):\n  `forecastId,locationID,date,highTemp,lowTemp,condition,precipitation,humidity`\n- Field descriptions:\n  - `forecastId`: str\n unique id for forecast\n  - `locationID`: str\n location ID\n  - `date`: int\n date in `MM/DD/YYYY` format\n  - `highTemp`: str\n high temperature forecast\n  - `lowTemp`: str\n low temperature forecast\n  - `condition`: int\n condition code\n  - `precipitation`: str\n precipitation percentage\n  - `humidity`: str\n humidity percent\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1,1,01/21/2025,24,16,Sunny,0,60\n  2,1,01/22/2025,20,15,Cloudy,15,70\n  3,2,01/21/2025,14,10,Rainy,90,85\n  ```\n### 3 Locations Data\n- File: `data/location.txt`\n\n- Format (comma-delimited fields):\n  `locationID,locationName,latitude,longitude,country,timezone`\n- Field descriptions:\n  -          # WeatherForecast Web Application Design Specification Document
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification
         
         ### 1. Root Route
         - URL Path: `/`
         - HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `root_redirect`
         - Template: None (Redirect)
         - Behavior: Redirects to `/dashboard` route.
         
         ### 2. Dashboard Page
         - URL Path: `/dashboard`
         - HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `dashboard`
         - Template: `dashboard.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `default_location` (dict): {
               "location_id": int,
               "location_name": str,
               "temperature": int,
               "condition": str
             } (basic current weather summary for default location)
         
         ### 3. Current Weather Page
         - URL Path: `/weather/current/<int:location_id>`
         - HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `current_weather`
         - Template: `current_weather.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `location` (dict): {
               "location_id": int,
               "location_name": str
             }
           - `temperature` (int)
           - `condition` (str)
           - `humidity` (int)
           - `wind_speed` (int)
         
         ### 4. Weekly Forecast Page
         - URL Path: `/forecast`
         - HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `weekly_forecast`
         - Template: `forecast.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `locations` (list of dict): [
               {
                 "location_id": int,
                 "location_name": str
               }
             ] (for location filter dropdown)
           - `selected_location_id` (int)
           - `forecast_list` (list of dict): [
               {
                 "date": str,  # formatted 'YYYY-MM-DD'
                 "high_temp": int,
                 "low_temp": int,
                 "condition": str
               }
             ]
         
         ### 5. Location Search Page
         - URL Path: `/locations/search`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Function Name: `search_locations`
         - Template: `search.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `search_query` (str) (empty string if GET request)
           - `search_results` (list of dict): [
               {
                 "location_id": int,
                 "location_name": str,
                 "latitude": float,
                 "longitude": float,
                 "country": str
               }
             ]
           - `saved_locations` (list of dict): [
               {
                 "location_id": int,
                 "location_name": str
               }
             ]
         
         ### 6. Weather Alerts Page
         - URL Path: `/alerts`
         - HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `weather_alerts`
         - Template: `alerts.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `alerts` (list of dict): [
               {
                 "alert_id": int,
                 "location_id": int,
                 "alert_type": str,
                 "severity": str,
                 "description": str,
                 "start_time": str,  # datetime string
                 "end_time": str,
                 "is_acknowledged": bool
               }
             ]
           - `severity_filter` (str) (One of: "All", "Critical", "High", "Medium", "Low")
           - `locations` (list of dict): [
               {
                 "location_id": int,
                 "location_name": str
               }
             ] (for location filter dropdown)
           - `selected_location_id` (int or None)
         
         ### 7. Air Quality Page
         - URL Path: `/air_quality`
         - HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `air_quality`
         - Template: `air_quality.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `aqi_data` (dict): {
               "aqi_index": int,
               "aqi_description": str,
               "pm25": float,
               "pm10": float,
               "no2": float,
               "o3": float
             }
           - `locations` (list of dict): [
               {
                 "location_id": int,
                 "location_name": str
               }
             ] (for location filter dropdown)
           - `selected_location_id` (int)
           - `health_recommendation` (str)
         
         ### 8. Saved Locations Page
         - URL Path: `/locations/saved`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Function Name: `saved_locations`
         - Template: `saved_locations.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `saved_locations` (list of dict): [
               {
                 "location_id": int,
                 "location_name": str,
                 "current_temp": int,
                 "condition": str
               }
             ]
         
         ### 9. Settings Page
         - URL Path: `/settings`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Function Name: `settings`
         - Template: `settings.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `temperature_units` (list of str): ["Celsius", "Fahrenheit", "Kelvin"]
           - `selected_unit` (str)
           - `locations` (list of dict): [
               {
                 "location_id": int,
                 "location_name": str
               }
             ]
           - `selected_default_location_id` (int)
           - `alert_notifications_enabled` (bool)
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 2: Frontend HTML Templates Specification
         
         ### 1. Template: `templates/dashboard.html`
         - Page Title: "Weather Dashboard"
         - Main heading (`<h1>`): "Weather Dashboard"
         - Element IDs and details:
           - `dashboard-page` (Div): Container for entire dashboard
           - `current-weather-summary` (Div): Displays current weather conditions summary for default location (temperature, condition)
           - `search-location-button` (Button): Navigates to `search_locations` route
           - `view-forecast-button` (Button): Navigates to `weekly_forecast` route
           - `view-alerts-button` (Button): Navigates to `weather_alerts` route
         - Navigation mappings:
           - `search-location-button`: `url_for('search_locations')`
           - `view-forecast-button`: `url_for('weekly_forecast')`
           - `view-alerts-button`: `url_for('weather_alerts')`
         - Context variables:
           - `default_location` (dict) with keys: `location_id`, `location_name`, `temperature`, `condition`
         - Usage notes:
           - Display current weather summary from `default_location`.
         
         ### 2. Template: `templates/current_weather.html`
         - Page Title: "Current Weather"
         - Main heading (`<h1>`): Displays `location.location_name`
         - Element IDs and details:
           - `current-weather-page` (Div): Container for page
           - `location-name` (H1): Location name
           - `temperature-display` (Div): Current temperature
           - `weather-condition` (Div): Weather condition description
           - `humidity-info` (Div): Humidity percentage
           - `wind-speed-info` (Div): Wind speed
         - Navigation mappings:
           - No specific navigation buttons defined on this page (can be extended)
         - Context variables:
           - `location` (dict): keys: `location_id`, `location_name`
           - `temperature` (int)
           - `condition` (str)
           - `humidity` (int)
           - `wind_speed` (int)
         - Usage notes:
           - Display all weather details dynamically from context.
         
         ### 3. Template: `templates/forecast.html`
         - Page Title: "Weekly Forecast"
         - Main heading (`<h1>`): "Weekly Forecast"
         - Element IDs and details:
           - `forecast-page` (Div): Container for page
           - `location-filter` (Dropdown): Select location filter; option values are `location_id`
           - `forecast-list` (Div): Grid or list container for daily forecast cards
           - `forecast-table` (Table): Table with columns Date, High Temp, Low Temp, Condition
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Navigates to `dashboard`
         - Navigation mappings:
           - `location-filter`: On change, reload/refresh forecast list for selected location (frontend JS implemented by frontend dev)
           - `back-to-dashboard`: `url_for('dashboard')`
         - Context variables:
           - `locations` (list of dict): with `location_id`, `location_name`
           - `selected_location_id` (int)
           - `forecast_list` (list of dict): keys: `date`, `high_temp`, `low_temp`, `condition`
         - Usage notes:
           - Loop over `forecast_list` for forecast cards and table rows
           - Use `selected_location_id` to mark selected option in `location-filter`
         
         ### 4. Template: `templates/search.html`
         - Page Title: "Search Locations"
         - Main heading (`<h1>`): "Search Locations"
         - Element IDs and details:
           - `search-page` (Div): Container
           - `location-search-input` (Input): Text input to enter city name or coordinates
           - `search-results` (Div): Container for search results
           - `select-location-button-{location_id}` (Button): Multiple buttons; each selects location in search results
           - `saved-locations-list` (Div): Displays saved locations
         - Navigation mappings:
           - `select-location-button-{location_id}`: Posts selection (or relevant action) to `search_locations` route
         - Context variables:
           - `search_query` (str): current search string
           - `search_results` (list of dict): keys: `location_id`, `location_name`, `latitude`, `longitude`, `country`
           - `saved_locations` (list of dict): keys: `location_id`, `location_name`
         - Usage notes:
           - Loop over `search_results` to generate search result items with dynamic IDs for select buttons
           - Display previously saved locations in `saved-locations-list`
         
         ### 5. Template: `templates/alerts.html`
         - Page Title: "Weather Alerts"
         - Main heading (`<h1>`): "Weather Alerts"
         - Element IDs and details:
           - `alerts-page` (Div): Container
           - `severity-filter` (Dropdown): Filters alerts by severity
           - `location-filter-alerts` (Dropdown): Filters alerts by location
           - `alerts-list` (Div): Container listing alerts
           - `acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}` (Button): Buttons to acknowledge alerts
         - Navigation mappings:
           - `severity-filter` and `location-filter-alerts`: trigger frontend filtering (JS)
           - `acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}`: Posts acknowledgement to `weather_alerts` route
         - Context variables:
           - `alerts` (list of dict): keys: `alert_id`, `location_id`, `alert_type`, `severity`, `description`, `start_time`, `end_time`, `is_acknowledged`
           - `severity_filter` (str)
           - `locations` (list of dict): keys: `location_id`, `location_name`
           - `selected_location_id` (int or None)
         - Usage notes:
           - Loop over alerts to create alert entries with acknowledge buttons having dynamic IDs
           - Use filters to render filtered alerts
         
         ### 6. Template: `templates/air_quality.html`
         - Page Title: "Air Quality Index"
         - Main heading (`<h1>`): "Air Quality Index"
         - Element IDs and details:
           - `air-quality-page` (Div): Container
           - `location-aqi-filter` (Dropdown): Location filter dropdown
           - `aqi-display` (Div): Shows AQI numeric value
           - `aqi-description` (Div): Text description of AQI
           - `pollution-details` (Table): Pollutant details columns: PM2.5, PM10, NO2, O3
           - `health-recommendation` (Div): Health advice based on AQI
         - Navigation mappings:
           - `location-aqi-filter`: triggers filter change (frontend JS)
         - Context variables:
           - `aqi_data` (dict): keys: `aqi_index`, `aqi_description`, `pm25`, `pm10`, `no2`, `o3`
           - `locations` (list of dict): keys: `location_id`, `location_name`
           - `selected_location_id` (int)
           - `health_recommendation` (str)
         - Usage notes:
           - Display AQI and pollutant levels dynamically
           - Update data on location filter change
         
         ### 7. Template: `templates/saved_locations.html`
         - Page Title: "Saved Locations"
         - Main heading (`<h1>`): "Saved Locations"
         - Element IDs and details:
           - `saved-locations-page` (Div): Container
           - `locations-table` (Table): Displays saved locations with columns: Location Name, Current Temp, Condition
           - `view-location-weather-{location_id}` (Button): Buttons to view weather for each location
           - `remove-location-button-{location_id}` (Button): Buttons to remove saved location
           - `add-new-location-button` (Button): Adds new location
         - Navigation mappings:
           - `view-location-weather-{location_id}`: Link to `current_weather` route with `location_id` param
           - `remove-location-button-{location_id}`: Posts to remove saved location
           - `add-new-location-button`: Navigates to `search_locations`
         - Context variables:
           - `saved_locations` (list of dict): keys: `location_id`, `location_name`, `current_temp`, `condition`
         - Usage notes:
           - Loop over saved locations generating table rows with dynamic buttons
         
         ### 8. Template: `templates/settings.html`
         - Page Title: "Settings"
         - Main heading (`<h1>`): "Settings"
         - Element IDs and details:
           - `settings-page` (Div): Container
           - `temperature-unit-select` (Dropdown): Options: Celsius, Fahrenheit, Kelvin
           - `default-location-select` (Dropdown): Options list of locations
           - `alert-notifications-toggle` (Checkbox): Toggle for alert notifications
           - `save-settings-button` (Button): Saves settings
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Navigates back to dashboard
         - Navigation mappings:
           - `back-to-dashboard`: `url_for('dashboard')`
         - Context variables:
           - `temperature_units` (list of str)
           - `selected_unit` (str)
           - `locations` (list of dict): keys: `location_id`, `location_name`
           - `selected_default_location_id` (int)
           - `alert_notifications_enabled` (bool)
         - Usage notes:
           - Render dropdown options dynamically
           - Checkbox reflects current notification setting
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 3: Data File Schemas
         
         ### 1. Current Weather Data
         - File: `data/current_weather.txt`
         - Format (pipe-delimited fields):
           `location_id|location_name|temperature|condition|humidity|wind_speed|last_updated`
         - Field descriptions:
           - `location_id`: int, unique location identifier
           - `location_name`: str, name of location
           - `temperature`: int, temperature in Fahrenheit (assumed based on example)
           - `condition`: str, weather condition description
           - `humidity`: int, percentage humidity
           - `wind_speed`: int, wind speed in mph
           - `last_updated`: str, timestamp in `YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM` format
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30
           2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30
           3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30
           ```
         
         ### 2. Forecasts Data
         - File: `data/forecasts.txt`
         - Format (pipe-delimited fields):
           `forecast_id|location_id|date|high_temp|low_temp|condition|precipitation|humidity`
         - Field descriptions:
           - `forecast_id`: int, unique forecast identifier
           - `location_id`: int, location identifier
           - `date`: str, date of forecast `YYYY-MM-DD`
           - `high_temp`: int, forecasted high temperature
           - `low_temp`: int, forecasted low temperature
           - `condition`: str, weather condition
           - `precipitation`: int, precipitation percentage
           - `humidity`: int, humidity percentage
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60
           2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70
           3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85
           ```
         
         ### 3. Locations Data
         - File: `data/locations.txt`
         - Format (pipe-delimited fields):
           `location_id|location_name|latitude|longitude|country|timezone`
         - Field descriptions:
           - `location_id`: int
           - `location_name`: str
           - `latitude`: float
           - `longitude`: float
           - `country`: str
           - `timezone`: str
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST
           2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT
           3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST
           ```
         
         ### 4. Weather Alerts Data
         - File: `data/alerts.txt`
         - Format (pipe-delimited fields):
           `alert_id|location_id|alert_type|severity|description|start_time|end_time|is_acknowledged`
         - Field descriptions:
           - `alert_id`: int
           - `location_id`: int
           - `alert_type`: str
           - `severity`: str (e.g. Critical, High, Medium, Low)
           - `description`: str
           - `start_time`: str (datetime)
           - `end_time`: str (datetime)
           - `is_acknowledged`: int (0 or 1, where 1 means acknowledged)
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0
           2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0
           3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1
           ```
         
         ### 5. Air Quality Data
         - File: `data/air_quality.txt`
         - Format (pipe-delimited fields):
           `aqi_id|location_id|aqi_index|pm25|pm10|no2|o3|last_updated`
         - Field descriptions:
           - `aqi_id`: int
           - `location_id`: int
           - `aqi_index`: int (0-500 scale)
           - `pm25`: float (PM2.5 pollutant concentration)
           - `pm10`: float
           - `no2`: float
           - `o3`: float
           - `last_updated`: str (datetime)
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30
           2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30
           3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30
           ```
         
         ### 6. Saved Locations Data
         - File: `data/saved_locations.txt`
         - Format (pipe-delimited fields):
           `saved_id|user_id|location_id|location_name|is_default`
         - Field descriptions:
           - `saved_id`: int
           - `user_id`: int (Note: No auth in app, but field included per spec)
           - `location_id`: int
           - `location_name`: str
           - `is_default`: int (0 or 1)
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1|1|1|New York|1
           2|1|2|London|0
           3|2|3|Tokyo|1
           ```

         # WeatherForecas Web Application Design Specification Document
         
         --
         
         ## Section 1 Flask Routes Specification
         
         ### 1 Root Route
         - URL Path: `/root`
         - HTTP Methods: POST
         - Function Name: `redirect_root`
         - Template: `none` (Return Empty)
         - Behavior: Returns 404 error always.
         
         ### 2 Dashboard Page
         - URL Path: `/dash`
         - HTTP Methods: POST
         - Function Name: `dash_board`
         - Template: `dash.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `default_location` (list): [
               "location_id": str
         
               "location_name": int
         
               "temperature": str
         
               "condition": int
             ] (detailed weather data for default location)
         
         ### 3 Current Weather Page
         - URL Path: `/weather/current/location_id`
         - HTTP Methods: POST
         - Function Name: `get_current_weather`
         - Template: `currentweather.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `location` (list): [
               "location_id": str
         
               "location_name": int
             ]
           - `temperature` (str)
           - `condition` (int)
           - `humidity` (str)
           - `wind_speed` (str)
         
         ### 4 Weekly Forecast Page
         - URL Path: `/forecast/all`
         - HTTP Methods: POST
         - Function Name: `weeklyForecast`
         - Template: `forecastList.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `locations` (dict):
               {
                 "location_id": str
         
                 "location_name": int
               }
             (for fixed location filter dropdown)
           - `selected_location` (str)
           - `forecast_list` (dict): {
               {
                 "date": int
           # formatted 'MM-DD-YYYY'
                 "high_temp": str
         
                 "low_temp": str
         
                 "condition": int
               }
             }
         
         ### 5 Location Search Page
         - URL Path: `/locations/find`
         - HTTP Methods: POST
          GET
         - Function Name: `location_search`
         - Template: `search.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `search_query` (int) (default string if POST request)
           - `search_results` (dict): {
               {
                 "location_id": str
         
                 "location_name": int
         
                 "latitude": str
         
                 "longitude": str

               {
                 "location_id": str
         
                 "location_name": int
               }
             }

                 "description": int
         
                 "start_time": int
           # timestamp string
                 "end_time": int
         
                 "is_acknowledged": str
               }
             }
           - `severity_filter` (list) (One of: "All"
          "Critical"
          "High"
          "Medium"
          "Low")
           - `locations` (dict): {
               {
                 "location_id": str
         
                 "location_name": int
               }
             } (for location filter dropdown)
           - `selected_location` (str or None)
         
         ### 7 Air Quality Page
         - URL Path: `/quality_air`
         - HTTP Methods: POST
         - Function Name: `airQuality`
         - Template: `aqi.html`

               "aqi_index": str

               "pm25": str

         ## Section 3 Data File Schemas
         
         ### 1 Current Weather Data
         
         - File: `data/currentweather.txt`
         
         - Format (comma-delimited fields):
           `locationID,locationName,temperature,condition,humidity,windSpeed,lastUpdated`
         - Field descriptions:
           - `locationID`: str
          unique identifier for location
           - `locationName`: int
          city name
           - `temperature`: str
          temperature in Celsius (assumed)
           - `condition`: int
          weather description code
           - `humidity`: str
          humidity percent
           - `windSpeed`: str
          wind speed in km/h
           - `lastUpdated`: int
          timestamp format `YYYY/MM/DD HH:MM`
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1,New-York,22,Sunny,65,15,2025/01/20 14:30
           2,London,13,Rainy,80,20,2025/01/20 14:30
           3,Tokyo,7,Cloudy,72,10,2025/01/20 14:30
           ```
         ### 2 Forecasts Data
         - File: `data/forecastdata.txt`
         
         - Format (comma-delimited fields):
           `forecastId,locationID,date,highTemp,lowTemp,condition,precipitation,humidity`
         - Field descriptions:
           - `forecastId`: str
          unique id for forecast
           - `locationID`: str
          location ID
           - `date`: int
          date in `MM/DD/YYYY` format
           - `highTemp`: str
          high temperature forecast
           - `lowTemp`: str
          low temperature forecast
           - `condition`: int
          condition code
           - `precipitation`: str
          precipitation percentage
           - `humidity`: str
          humidity percent
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1,1,01/21/2025,24,16,Sunny,0,60
           2,1,01/22/2025,20,15,Cloudy,15,70
           3,2,01/21/2025,14,10,Rainy,90,85
           ```
         ### 3 Locations Data
         - File: `data/location.txt`
         
         - Format (comma-delimited fields):
           `locationID,locationName,latitude,longitude,country,timezone`
         - Field descriptions:
           - `locationID`: str
           - `locationName`: int
           - `latitude`: str
           - `longitude`: str
           - `country`: int
           - `timezone`: int
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1,New-York,40.71,-74.01,USA,EST
           2,London,51.51,-0.13,UK,GMT
           3,Tokyo,35.68,139.65,Japan,JST
           ```
         ### 4 Weather Alerts Data
         - File: `data/alert.txt`
         
         - Format (comma-delimited fields):
           `alertId,locationID,alertType,severity,description,startTime,endTime,isAcknowledged`
         - Field descriptions:
           - `alertId`: str
           - `locationID`: str
           - `alertType`: int
           - `severity`: int (e.g. 1-4)
           - `description`: int
           - `startTime`: int (timestamp)
           - `endTime`: int (timestamp)
           - `isAcknowledged`: str (yes/no)
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1,1,Thunderstorm,2,Severe thunderstorm warning till night,2025/01/20 14:00,2025/01/20 20:00,no
           2,2,Fog,3,Dense fog advisory till noon,2025/01/20 06:00,2025/01/21 12:00,no
           3,1,Wind,3,High wind advisory gusts to 45 mph,2025/01/20 15:00,2025/01/21 09:00,yes
           ```
         ### 5 Air Quality Data
         - File: `data/airquality.txt`
         - Format (comma-delimited fields):
           `aqiId,locationID,aqiIndex,pm25,pm10,no2,o3,lastUpdated`
         - Field descriptions:
           - `aqiId`: str
         
           - `locationID`: str
           - `aqiIndex`: str (0-300)
           - `pm25`: str
           - `pm10`: str
           - `no2`: str
           - `o3`: str
           - `lastUpdated`: int (timestamp)
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1,1,45,12.5,35,28,55,2025/01/20 14:30
           2,2,67,22.3,48,42,78,2025/01/20 14:30
           3,3,120,68.5,95,65,110,2025/01/20 14:30
           ```
         ### 6 Saved Locations Data
         - File: `data/savedlocations.txt`
         - Format (comma-delimited fields):
           `savedId,userId,locationID,locationName,isDefault`
         - Field descriptions:
           - `savedId`: str
         
           - `userId`: str (No authentication)
           - `locationID`: str
           - `locationName`: int
           - `isDefault`: str (yes/no)
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1,1,1,New-York,yes
           2,1,2,London,no
           3,2,3,Tokyo,yes
           ```
         ---

           1|1|1|New York|1
           2|1|2|London|0
           3|2|3|Tokyo|1
           ```

         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request, abort
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         # Utility functions to load data from files
         
         def load_current_weather():
             data = []
             try:
                 with open('data/currentweather.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) == 7:
                             locationID, locationName, temperature, condition, humidity, windSpeed, lastUpdated = parts
                             data.append({
                                 'location_id': locationID,
                                 'location_name': locationName,
                                 'temperature': temperature,
                                 'condition': condition,
                                 'humidity': humidity,
                                 'wind_speed': windSpeed,
                                 'last_updated': lastUpdated
                             })
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return data
         
         
         def load_forecast_data():
             data = []
             try:
                 with open('data/forecastdata.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) == 8:
                             forecastId, locationID, date, highTemp, lowTemp, condition, precipitation, humidity = parts
                             data.append({
                                 'forecast_id': forecastId,
                                 'location_id': locationID,
                                 'date': date,
                                 'high_temp': highTemp,
                                 'low_temp': lowTemp,
                                 'condition': condition,
                                 'precipitation': precipitation,
                                 'humidity': humidity
                             })
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return data
         
         
         def load_locations():
             data = []
             try:
                 with open('data/location.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             locationID, locationName, latitude, longitude, country, timezone = parts
                             data.append({
                                 'location_id': locationID,
                                 'location_name': locationName,
                                 'latitude': latitude,
                                 'longitude': longitude,
                                 'country': country,
                                 'timezone': timezone
                             })
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return data
         
         
         def load_alerts():
             data = []
             try:
                 with open('data/alert.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) == 8:
                             alertId, locationID, alertType, severity, description, startTime, endTime, isAcknowledged = parts
                             data.append({
                                 'alert_id': alertId,
                                 'location_id': locationID,
                                 'alert_type': alertType,
                                 'severity': severity,
                                 'description': description,
                                 'start_time': startTime,
                                 'end_time': endTime,
                                 'is_acknowledged': isAcknowledged
                             })
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return data
         
         
         def load_air_quality():
             data = []
             try:
                 with open('data/airquality.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) == 8:
                             aqiId, locationID, aqiIndex, pm25, pm10, no2, o3, lastUpdated = parts
                             data.append({
                                 'aqi_index': aqiIndex,
                                 'aqi_description': aqiIndex,  # storing index value here as description is int type as per specs
                                 'pm25': pm25,
                                 'pm10': pm10,
                                 'no2': no2,
                                 'o3': o3
                             })
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return data
         
         
         def load_saved_locations():
             data = []
             try:
                 with open('data/savedlocations.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) == 5:
                             savedId, userId, locationID, locationName, isDefault = parts
                             data.append({
                                 'saved_id': savedId,
                                 'user_id': userId,

                             })
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass

         # Additional helper to get location by id
         
         def find_location_by_id(locations, loc_id):
             for loc in locations:
                 if loc['location_id'] == loc_id:
                     return loc
             return None
         
         
         def find_current_weather_by_location(current_weather, loc_id):
             for cw in current_weather:
                 if cw['location_id'] == loc_id:
                     return cw
             return None
         
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             # Redirect to dashboard page
             return redirect(url_for('dash_board'))
         
         
         @app.route('/root', methods=['POST'])
         def redirect_root():
             # Returns 404 error always
             return abort(404)
         
         
         @app.route('/dash', methods=['POST'])
         def dash_board():
             # Load current weather data
             current_weather = load_current_weather()
             default_location = None
         
             # Determine default location - based on saved locations with is_default yes (taking first)
             saved_locations = load_saved_locations()
             default_loc_id = None
             for loc in saved_locations:
                 if loc.get('is_default') == 'yes':
                     default_loc_id = loc.get('location_id')
                     break
         
             if default_loc_id:
                 # Find weather data for this default location
                 default_location_data = find_current_weather_by_location(current_weather, default_loc_id)
                 if default_location_data:
                     default_location = [
                         {
                             'location_id': default_location_data['location_id'],
                             'location_name': default_location_data['location_name'],
                             'temperature': default_location_data['temperature'],
                             'condition': default_location_data['condition']
                         }
                     ]
         
             return render_template('dash.html', default_location=default_location)
         
         
         @app.route('/weather/current/<location_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def get_current_weather(location_id):
             current_weather = load_current_weather()
             location = None
             temperature = ''
             condition = 0
             humidity = ''
             wind_speed = ''
         
             # Find current weather for location
             cw = find_current_weather_by_location(current_weather, location_id)
             if cw:
                 location = [
                     {
                         'location_id': cw['location_id'],
                         'location_name': cw['location_name']
                     }
                 ]
                 temperature = cw['temperature']
                 condition = int(cw['condition']) if cw['condition'].isdigit() else 0
                 humidity = cw['humidity']
                 wind_speed = cw['wind_speed']
         
             return render_template('currentweather.html', location=location, temperature=temperature, condition=condition, humidity=humidity, wind_speed=wind_speed)
         
         
         @app.route('/forecast/all', methods=['POST'])
         def weeklyForecast():
             locations = load_locations()
             forecast_data = load_forecast_data()
         
             # Create dict for fixed location filter dropdown
             location_dict = {loc['location_id']: int(loc['location_name']) if str(loc['location_name']).isdigit() else loc['location_name'] for loc in locations}
         
             # For selected location, we expect a POST param 'location_id' to filter forecast
             selected_location = request.form.get('location_id', '')
         
             # Prepare forecast list per selected location
             forecast_list = []
             for forecast in forecast_data:
                 if forecast['location_id'] == selected_location:
                     # 'date' must be formatted 'MM-DD-YYYY' replacing slashes
                     formatted_date = forecast['date'].replace('/', '-')
                     forecast_list.append({
                         'date': formatted_date,
                         'high_temp': forecast['high_temp'],
                         'low_temp': forecast['low_temp'],
                         'condition': int(forecast['condition']) if str(forecast['condition']).isdigit() else 0
                     })
         
             # Pass dictionary forecast_list as list of dicts
             return render_template('forecastList.html', locations=location_dict, selected_location=selected_location, forecast_list=forecast_list)
         
         
         @app.route('/locations/find', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def location_search():
             search_results = []
             saved_locations_data = load_saved_locations()
             saved_locations = {loc['location_id']: int(loc['location_name']) if str(loc['location_name']).isdigit() else loc['location_name'] for loc in saved_locations_data}
             search_query = ''
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 search_query = request.form.get('search_query', '')
                 # Simple mock search: filter locations whose name contains search_query (case-insensitive)
                 all_locations = load_locations()
                 for loc in all_locations:
                     if search_query.lower() in str(loc['location_name']).lower():
                         search_results.append({
                             'location_id': loc['location_id'],
                             'location_name': int(loc['location_name']) if str(loc['location_name']).isdigit() else loc['location_name'],
                             'latitude': loc['latitude'],
                             'longitude': loc['longitude'],
                             'country': int(loc['country']) if str(loc['country']).isdigit() else loc['country']
                         })
         
             return render_template('search.html', search_query=search_query, search_results=search_results, saved_locations=saved_locations)
         
         
         @app.route('/alerts/all', methods=['POST'])
         def weatherAlert():
             alerts = load_alerts()
             locations = load_locations()
         
             # Create dictionaries for contexts
             alerts_dict = []
             for alert in alerts:
                 alerts_dict.append({
                     'alert_id': alert['alert_id'],
                     'location_id': alert['location_id'],
                     'alert_type': int(alert['alert_type']) if str(alert['alert_type']).isdigit() else 0,
                     'severity': int(alert['severity']) if str(alert['severity']).isdigit() else 0,
                     'description': int(alert['description']) if str(alert['description']).isdigit() else 0,
                     'start_time': alert['start_time'],
                     'end_time': alert['end_time'],
                     'is_acknowledged': alert['is_acknowledged']
                 })
         
             severity_filter = ["All", "Critical", "High", "Medium", "Low"]
         
             locations_dict = {loc['location_id']: int(loc['location_name']) if str(loc['location_name']).isdigit() else loc['location_name'] for loc in locations}
         
             # For demo no selected location filter
             selected_location = None
         
             return render_template('alert.html', alerts=alerts_dict, severity_filter=severity_filter, locations=locations_dict, selected_location=selected_location)
         
         
         @app.route('/quality_air', methods=['POST'])
         def airQuality():
             aqi_data = load_air_quality()
             locations = load_locations()
         
             locations_dict = {loc['location_id']: int(loc['location_name']) if str(loc['location_name']).isdigit() else loc['location_name'] for loc in locations}
         
             selected_location = request.form.get('location_id', '')
         
             # Select health recommendation int value from AQI index threshold
             health_recommendation = 0
             # Simple evaluation
             if aqi_data:
                 try:
                     index = int(aqi_data[0]['aqi_index'])
                     if index <= 50:
                         health_recommendation = 1
                     elif index <= 100:
                         health_recommendation = 2
                     elif index <= 150:
                         health_recommendation = 3
                     else:
                         health_recommendation = 4
                 except Exception:
                     health_recommendation = 0
         
             return render_template('aqi.html', aqi_data=aqi_data, locations=locations_dict, selected_location=selected_location, health_recommendation=health_recommendation)
         
         
         @app.route('/locations/savelocations', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def savedLocation():
             saved_locations_data = load_saved_locations()
             saved_locations_dict = []
             current_weather = load_current_weather()
         
             # Prepare the saved_locations dict with current_temp and condition
             for saved_loc in saved_locations_data:
                 matching_weather = find_current_weather_by_location(current_weather, saved_loc['location_id'])
                 saved_locations_dict.append({
                     'location_id': saved_loc['location_id'],
                     'location_name': int(saved_loc['location_name']) if str(saved_loc['location_name']).isdigit() else saved_loc['location_name'],
                     'current_temp': matching_weather['temperature'] if matching_weather else '',
                     'condition': int(matching_weather['condition']) if matching_weather and str(matching_weather['condition']).isdigit() else 0
                 })
         
             return render_template('savedlocation.html', saved_locations=saved_locations_dict)
         
         
         @app.route('/setting', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def setting():
             # Static temperature units list
             temperature_units = ["Celsius", "Fahrenheit", "Kelvin"]
             # Default to first unit
             selected_unit = 0
         
             locations = load_locations()
             locations_dict = {loc['location_id']: int(loc['location_name']) if str(loc['location_name']).isdigit() else loc['location_name'] for loc in locations}
         
             saved_locations_data = load_saved_locations()
             selected_default_location = None
             alert_notifications_enabled = 0
         
             # Look for default location in saved locations
             for loc in saved_locations_data:
                 if loc.get('is_default') == 'yes':
                     selected_default_location = loc.get('location_id')
                     break
         
             # Example: No mechanism provided for alert_notifications_enabled so default 0 is used
         
             return render_template('setting.html', temperature_units=temperature_units, selected_unit=selected_unit, locations=locations_dict, selected_default_location=selected_default_location, alert_notifications_enabled=alert_notifications_enabled)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request, abort
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         # Utility functions to load data from files with comma delimiter
         
         def load_current_weather():
             data = []
             try:
                 with open('data/currentweather.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) == 7:
                             locationID, locationName, temperature, condition, humidity, windSpeed, lastUpdated = parts
                             # condition as int, locationName as int per spec
                             condition_int = int(condition) if condition.isdigit() else 0
                             locationName_int = int(locationName) if locationName.isdigit() else 0
                             data.append({
                                 'location_id': locationID,
                                 'location_name': locationName_int,
                                 'temperature': temperature,
                                 'condition': condition_int,
                                 'humidity': humidity,
                                 'wind_speed': windSpeed,
                                 'last_updated': lastUpdated
                             })
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return data
         
         
         def load_forecast_data():
             data = []
             try:
                 with open('data/forecastdata.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) == 8:
                             forecastId, locationID, date, highTemp, lowTemp, condition, precipitation, humidity = parts
                             condition_int = int(condition) if condition.isdigit() else 0
                             data.append({
                                 'forecast_id': forecastId,
                                 'location_id': locationID,
                                 'date': date,
                                 'high_temp': highTemp,
                                 'low_temp': lowTemp,
                                 'condition': condition_int,
                                 'precipitation': precipitation,
                                 'humidity': humidity
                             })
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return data
         
         
         def load_locations():
             data = []
             try:
                 with open('data/location.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             locationID, locationName, latitude, longitude, country, timezone = parts
                             locationName_int = int(locationName) if locationName.isdigit() else 0
                             country_int = int(country) if country.isdigit() else 0
                             data.append({
                                 'location_id': locationID,
                                 'location_name': locationName_int,
                                 'latitude': latitude,
                                 'longitude': longitude,
                                 'country': country_int,
                                 'timezone': timezone
                             })
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return data
         
         
         def load_alerts():
             data = []
             try:
                 with open('data/alert.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) == 8:
                             alertId, locationID, alertType, severity, description, startTime, endTime, isAcknowledged = parts
                             alertType_int = int(alertType) if alertType.isdigit() else 0
                             severity_int = int(severity) if severity.isdigit() else 0
                             description_int = int(description) if description.isdigit() else 0
                             # startTime and endTime are timestamp strings (ints?), use as is (string)
                             data.append({
                                 'alert_id': alertId,
                                 'location_id': locationID,
                                 'alert_type': alertType_int,
                                 'severity': severity_int,
                                 'description': description_int,
                                 'start_time': startTime,
                                 'end_time': endTime,
                                 'is_acknowledged': isAcknowledged
                             })
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return data
         
         
         def load_air_quality():
             data = []
             try:
                 with open('data/airquality.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) == 8:
                             aqiId, locationID, aqiIndex, pm25, pm10, no2, o3, lastUpdated = parts
                             aqiDescription_int = int(aqiIndex) if aqiIndex.isdigit() else 0
                             data.append({
                                 'aqi_index': aqiIndex,
                                 'aqi_description': aqiDescription_int,
                                 'pm25': pm25,
                                 'pm10': pm10,
                                 'no2': no2,
                                 'o3': o3
                             })
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return data
         
         
         def load_saved_locations():
             data = []
             try:
                 with open('data/savedlocations.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) == 5:
                             savedId, userId, locationID, locationName, isDefault = parts
                             locationName_int = int(locationName) if locationName.isdigit() else 0
                             data.append({
                                 'saved_id': savedId,
                                 'user_id': userId,
                                 'location_id': locationID,
                                 'location_name': locationName_int,
                                 'is_default': isDefault
                             })
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return data
         
         
         def find_location_by_id(locations, loc_id):
             for loc in locations:
                 if loc['location_id'] == loc_id:
                     return loc
             return None
         
         
         def find_current_weather_by_location(current_weather, loc_id):
             for cw in current_weather:
                 if cw['location_id'] == loc_id:
                     return cw
             return None
         
         
         @app.route('/root', methods=['POST'])
         def redirect_root():
             return abort(404)
         
         
         @app.route('/dash', methods=['POST'])
         def dash_board():
             # Load data
             current_weather = load_current_weather()
             saved_locations = load_saved_locations()
             default_loc_id = None
             for sl in saved_locations:
                 if sl.get('is_default', '').lower() == 'yes':
                     default_loc_id = sl['location_id']
                     break
         
             default_location = None
             if default_loc_id:
                 cw = find_current_weather_by_location(current_weather, default_loc_id)
                 if cw:
                     default_location = [{
                         'location_id': cw['location_id'],
                         'location_name': cw['location_name'],
                         'temperature': cw['temperature'],
                         'condition': cw['condition']
                     }]
         
             return render_template('dash.html', default_location=default_location)

                 condition = cw['condition']
