                                 'pm10': pm10,
                                 'no2': no2,
                                 'o3': o3
                             })
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return data
         
         
         def load_saved_locations():
             data = []
             try:
                 with open('data/savedlocations.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) == 5:
                             savedId, userId, locationID, locationName, isDefault = parts
                             location_name_int = int(locationName) if locationName.isdigit() else 0
                             data.append({
                                 'saved_id': savedId,
                                 'user_id': userId,
                                 'location_id': locationID,
                                 'location_name': location_name_int,
                                 'is_default': isDefault
                             })
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return data
         
         
         def find_location_by_id(locations, loc_id):
             for loc in locations:
                 if loc['location_id'] == loc_id:
                     return loc
             return None
         
         
         def find_current_weather_by_location(current_weather, loc_id):
             for cw in current_weather:
                 if cw['location_id'] == loc_id:
                     return cw
             return None
         
         
         @app.route('/root', methods=['POST'])
         def redirect_root():
             return abort(404)
         
         
         @app.route('/dash', methods=['POST'])
         def dash_board():
             current_weather = load_current_weather()
             saved_locations = load_saved_locations()
             default_loc_id = None
             for loc in saved_locations:
                 if loc.get('is_default', '').lower() == 'yes':
                     default_loc_id = loc['location_id']
                     break
         
             default_location = None
             if default_loc_id:
                 cw = find_current_weather_by_location(current_weather, default_loc_id)
                 if cw:
                     default_location = [{
                         'location_id': cw['location_id'],
                         'location_name': cw['location_name'],
                         'temperature': cw['temperature'],
                         'condition': cw['condition']
                     }]
         
             return render_template('dash.html', default_location=default_location)
         
         
         @app.route('/weather/current/<location_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def get_current_weather(location_id):
             current_weather = load_current_weather()
             cw = find_current_weather_by_location(current_weather, location_id)
         
             location = None
             temperature = ''
             condition = 0
             humidity = ''
             wind_speed = ''
             if cw:
                 location = [{
                     'location_id': cw['location_id'],
                     'location_name': cw['location_name']
                 }]
                 temperature = cw['temperature']
                 condition = cw['condition']
                 humidity = cw['humidity']
                 wind_speed = cw['wind_speed']
         
             return render_template('currentweather.html', location=location, temperature=temperature, condition=condition, humidity=humidity, wind_speed=wind_speed)
         
         
         @app.route('/forecast/all', methods=['POST'])
         def weeklyForecast():
             locations = load_locations()
             forecast_data = load_forecast_data()
         
             locations_dict = {loc['location_id']: loc['location_name'] for loc in locations}
         
             selected_location = request.form.get('location_id', '')
         
             forecast_list = []
             for f in forecast_data:
                 if f['location_id'] == selected_location:
                     date_fmt = f['date'].replace('/', '-')
                     forecast_list.append({
                         'date': date_fmt,
                         'high_temp': f['high_temp'],
                         'low_temp': f['low_temp'],
                         'condition': f['condition']
                     })
         
             return render_template('forecastList.html', locations=locations_dict, selected_location=selected_location, forecast_list=forecast_list)
         
         
         @app.route('/locations/find', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def location_search():
             search_query = ''
             search_results = []
             saved_locations_data = load_saved_locations()
             saved_locations = {loc['location_id']: loc['location_name'] for loc in saved_locations_data}
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 search_query = request.form.get('search_query', '')
                 all_locations = load_locations()
                 for loc in all_locations:
                     if search_query.lower() in str(loc['location_name']).lower():
                         search_results.append({
                             'location_id': loc['location_id'],
                             'location_name': loc['location_name'],
                             'latitude': loc['latitude'],
                             'longitude': loc['longitude'],
                             'country': loc['country']
                         })
         
             return render_template('search.html', search_query=search_query, search_results=search_results, saved_locations=saved_locations)
         
         
         @app.route('/alerts/all', methods=['POST'])
         def weatherAlert():
             alerts = load_alerts()
             locations = load_locations()
         
             alerts_dict = []
             for alert in alerts:
                 alerts_dict.append({
                     'alert_id': alert['alert_id'],
                     'location_id': alert['location_id'],
                     'alert_type': alert['alert_type'],
                     'severity': alert['severity'],
                     'description': alert['description'],
                     'start_time': alert['start_time'],
                     'end_time': alert['end_time'],
                     'is_acknowledged': alert['is_acknowledged']
                 })
         
             severity_filter = ["All", "Critical", "High", "Medium", "Low"]
             locations_dict = {loc['location_id']: loc['location_name'] for loc in locations}
             selected_location = None
         
             return render_template('alert.html', alerts=alerts_dict, severity_filter=severity_filter, locations=locations_dict, selected_location=selected_location)
         
         
         @app.route('/quality_air', methods=['POST'])
         def airQuality():
             aqi_data = load_air_quality()
             locations = load_locations()
         
             locations_dict = {loc['location_id']: loc['location_name'] for loc in locations}
         
             selected_location = request.form.get('location_id', '')
         
             health_recommendation = 0
             if aqi_data:
                 try:
                     idx = int(aqi_data[0]['aqi_index'])
                     if idx <= 50:
                         health_recommendation = 1
                     elif idx <= 100:
                         health_recommendation = 2
                     elif idx <= 150:
                         health_recommendation = 3
                     else:
                         health_recommendation = 4
                 except Exception:
                     health_recommendation = 0
         
             return render_template('aqi.html', aqi_data=aqi_data, locations=locations_dict, selected_location=selected_location, health_recommendation=health_recommendation)
         
         
         @app.route('/locations/savelocations', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def savedLocation():
             saved_locations_data = load_saved_locations()
             current_weather = load_current_weather()
         
             saved_locations_dict = []
             for saved_loc in saved_locations_data:
                 cw = find_current_weather_by_location(current_weather, saved_loc['location_id'])
                 saved_locations_dict.append({
                     'location_id': saved_loc['location_id'],
                     'location_name': saved_loc['location_name'],
                     'current_temp': cw['temperature'] if cw else '',
                     'condition': cw['condition'] if cw else 0
                 })
         
             return render_template('savedlocation.html', saved_locations=saved_locations_dict)
         
         
         @app.route('/setting', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def setting():
             temperature_units = ["Celsius", "Fahrenheit", "Kelvin"]
         
             selected_unit = 0
             locations = load_locations()
             locations_dict = {loc['location_id']: loc['location_name'] for loc in locations}
         
             saved_locations = load_saved_locations()
             selected_default_location = None
             alert_notifications_enabled = 0
         
             for sl in saved_locations:
                 if sl.get('is_default', '').lower() == 'yes':
                     selected_default_location = sl['location_id']
                     break
         
             return render_template('setting.html', temperature_units=temperature_units, selected_unit=selected_unit, locations=locations_dict, selected_default_location=selected_default_location, alert_notifications_enabled=alert_notifications_enabled)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True, port=5000)
